    (local.get $3)
   )
   ;; code offset: 0x641

     ;; code offset: 0x63a
     (i32.const 1024)
     ;; code offset: 0x63d

    )

  )

   ;; code offset: 0x647

    ;; code offset: 0x643
    (local.get $8)
    ;; code offset: 0x645
    (i32.const 32)
   )
  )

  (local.get $5)
